Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageDanbury Senior Living contact form
URLhttps://www.danburyseniorliving.com/surveys/schedule-a-tour
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Score1703
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1703, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 612. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

solos: Score 26. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 98

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test region, score 21 (Some page content is not contained by landmarks)
  • Package ibm, test Rpt_Aria_OrphanedContent_Native_Host_Sematics, score 88 (Content does not reside within an element with a landmark role)

Issue menuNavigation

WCAG: 2.1.1

Score: 92

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test menuNav, score 90 (Nonstandard keyboard navigation among focusable menu items)

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 90

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 86 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 4 (Element has insufficient color contrast)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 74

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 10 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 68 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
